class=\"textplan\">\n\t\t\t\t<h1>Do I Qualify for a Plan?</h1>\n\t\t\t\t<p>In order to get an Obamacare Plan, you must sign up during <a href=\"https://www.obamacareplans.com/enrollment-periods/open-enrollment\" class=\"kt-link\">Open Enrollment</a>. If you missed Open Enrollment, you can still get an Obamacare plan during <a href=\"https://www.obamacareplans.com/enrollment-periods/special-enrollment\" class=\"kt-link\">Special Enrollment</a>. You qualify for Special Enrollment if you, or someone in your household, recently experienced certain life events -- such as login health coverage, changing jobs, getting marriend/divorced, having a child, or moving, to name a few.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class=\"qcarrusel\">\n\t\t\t\t<div id=\"logosqualify\" class=\"mainGrid\">\n\t\t\t\t    \n\t\t\t\t    <div Care Act (ACA), also known as \"<a href=\"https://www.obamacareplans.com/learn/common-questions/?&amp;ds=aca\" class=\"kt-link-white\">Obamacare</a>\", has helped millions of people get health care coverage. Before the ACA, health insurance was unaffordable and unavailable for many. Now, with Obamacare, if you meet certain <a href=\"https://www.obamacareplans.com/qualifying-for-lower-costs\" class=\"kt-link-white\">qualifications</a>, the government will help pay for your monthly premiums and out-of-pocket cost. And for those who have preexisting medical conditions, you can no longer be denied coverage under Obamacare.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"imgcareact\">\n\t\t\t\t<img src=\"//images.katch.com/sem/ocp/get-quotes/v12/images/act.png\" alt=\"Care Acts\">\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t   <div class=\"clear\"></div>\n\t</div>\n\t<div class=\"cwhychoose\">\n\t\t<div class=\"whychoose\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"titlewhychoose\">Why Choose ObamacarePlans.com</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"contentwhychoose\">\n\t\t\t\t<p>We are <a href=\"https://www.obamacareplans.com/learn/common-questions\" class=\"kt-link\">not the government</a>.
